<p><a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener" class="external text" href="http://onegame.gg/">One Game Agency</a> returns with season 3 of  <b>AMD SAPPHIRE OGA Dota PIT EU/CIS</b>, featuring some of the best European and CIS teams as they compete for the $170,000 <abbr title="United States Dollar">USD</abbr> prize pool.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Format">Format</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=Dota_Pit_League/Online/3/Europe_CIS&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Format">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b>Participants</b>
<ul><li>Six invited teams</li>
<li>Two teams from a <a href="/dota2/Dota_Pit_League/Online/3/Europe_CIS/Closed_Qualifier" title="Dota Pit League/Online/3/Europe CIS/Closed Qualifier">closed qualifier</a></li></ul></li>
<li><b>Playoffs</b>
<ul><li>Double-elimination bracket</li>
<li>All matches except Grand Final are <abbr title="Best-of-three">Bo3</abbr></li>
<li>Grand Final is <abbr title="Best-of-five">Bo5</abbr></li></ul></li></ul>
